| Use Case 1: Puja Services | Buyer raises a request for Puja services on a buyer app → Seller responds with available Pujari details and Puja options → Buyer selects a Puja and Pujari → Seller confirms the appointment → Puja is conducted as per the chosen details.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |     | Seller (one with the inventory) |     | Buyer app |     | Seller app\*\* |
| Main Path                 | **Thought** Puja services offer individuals a way to engage in spiritual practices from the comfort of their homes or preferred locations. ONDC is committed to making these services interoperable, ensuring easy access and availability of various Pujas to cater to diverse spiritual needs. **Initiate Buyer’s Request** Buyer’s request for any Spirituality related product can be raised through the buyer app in three possible ways: Search through category: Buyer can easily search for the category directly such as Puja Services Search by city: Buyer app can raise a search request by city for eg. all sellers selling only in Lucknow This search can be specific to fulfilment type ie. buyer fulfilled service or seller fulfilled service that the seller can define at the time of sending across the catalogue and the buyer can choose based on the options available for their location. For explanation purposes, search by category is defined here. Search by category Buyer on the buyer app raises an intent to purchase a spirituality service of either of the following, Puja Services Astrology Services The buyer can raise an intent of either one of the above or all of the above categories of spirituality services available **Broadcast to Sellers** The interest is broadcasted to all the available sellers in the specific domain on the ONDC network via the gateway **Seller responds with their catalogue** Sellers will respond with their catalogues with **attributes** for the buyer app to define the discovery experience for the buyer. These attributes will be needed as selection from the buyer to define the quote of a purchasable item. The different attributes defined are: Name of Pooja Specify the name of Puja eg. Maha Mritunjay Path Capacity for the Puja How many people would be attending the Puja. Let’s say a single person, or a couple or a complete family of 4 people or more people This will be defined from the seller’s end. Possible values for the attribute can be single person, a couple or family of two, family of four and so on. Slots available Sellers will respond with the available slots which can specify date, time and service for the Puja. For example Maha Mritunjay Puja can be performed on 6th October from 4pm to 6pm Date of the Puja Time of the Puja Duration of the Puja How long the Puja will take place for? Duration of subscription: The duration will be defined in the ISO format to enable a user to specify and answer- how long any particular subscription is needed for? P is the duration designator (for period) placed at the start of the duration representation. Y is the year designator that follows the value for the number of years. M is the month designator that follows the value for the number of months. W is the week designator that follows the value for the number of weeks. D is the day designator that follows the value for the number of days. T is the time designator that precedes the time components of the representation. 1 month duration can be presented as **P1M** 48 hours duration can be presented as **PT48H** 6 months duration can be presented as **P6M** Location of Puja The seller will define the available locations for the Puja according to their catalogue Seller defined location: Puja being performed at the temple Buyer defined location: Seller provides the option to the buyer to choose the location. For eg. buyer’s home In case the Puja is being performed at the Temple, Temple details will be mentioned as Temple Description. Fulfilment type Online Puja: the Puja would be attended by the user in an online setup over a video call. Seller can send this as a part of the catalogue if the same service is offered by the seller Offline Puja: Where there is location selection for puja offline, be it the seller’s location(Temple) or Pujari specified location or buyer specified location Buyer fulfilled service: Seller can provide the option of buyer choosing the location Seller fulfilled service: Puja being performed at the temple Both online and offline Puja: Where the seller can offer services at the location of the seller/buyer and also send the video of the puja after completion Add ons Add-ons such as a Potli or some Yantra which would be provided along with the Puja can be specified in this attribute. These will be paid add ons and would have a monetary value attached to it. There can also be free add ons as a consultation astrology paper that is being provided free of cost along with the service Other attributes for sending the detailed catalogue for the buyer app to create the right experience for the buyer will be as below. Service or Concern: Sellers can respond with Service or Concern to specify the type of Puja services they offer, such as career related Puja or Relationship Related Puja These will be enums as defined below: Career Marriage Love Energy Home Education Job Pujari for the Puja: Sellers can respond with a list of Pujaris based on their Specialties that the Pujari supports Seller defined ratings and Experience of the Pujari Certifications available for the Pujari Pujari’s photo can also be passed as an added attribute for the buyer to take an informed decision Language of Pujari: Sellers can respond with languages that the Pandit speaks based on preferred languages (e.g., Hindi, English, Kannada) Experience of Pujari: Sellers can respond with the experience level of each Pandit, helping them select a knowledgeable professional. This can be in years eg. 10+ years, 12+ years Education/Qualification of Pujari: Any eligibility certification can be specified for this attribute Form for User Details: A form to collect necessary user information can be shared by the seller (e.g., name, contact number, birth details, Gotra) Image of Pooja: This can also be passed as a part of seller’s catalogue Description of Puja: Any further details related to the Puja that the seller deems fit for the user to be aware of can be passed in this attribute. For eg. for Rin Mukti Puja: A very remarkable and beneficial Puja to remove all debts is held in Ujjain's ancient Rinmukteshwar Mahadev Temple. In this worship, yellow objects are offered to Mahadev. According to history, during the Satayuga period, King Harishchandra himself performed this ritual in order to pay off his debts. Credentials of Poojari Any certificates that the Seller app understands are important to verify the authenticity for the seller can be added for this attribute Certificate name Certification number to check the authenticity Rating from seller Seller can pass the rating related to the any puja so that the buyer can take an informed decision regarding the same Checklist for the Puja: The seller can also send a checklist as part of the Puja. For eg. if a Puja has to be done at an individual’s home, Gangajal, Janeyu can be some specific items that need to be available for the Puja **Offer Management & Selection** Buyer will select the most suitable puja that they deem fit for their usage from all seller Apps catalogue Different models to be present for selection as received in the catalogue sent by the seller. Scenario 1: **Offline fulfilment model** Let’s suppose the seller app offers offline consumption of Puja ie. Puja being held at either the seller’s location(Temple) or buyer’s location(Home) The buyer app will have to provide details related to the selection for the seller to provide a quote. This will include Offline Puja: Where there is location selection for puja offline, be it the seller’s location(Temple) or Pujari specified location or buyer specified location Buyer fulfilled puja: Pujari visiting home for Puja Seller fulfilled puja: Buyer visiting the temple for Puja Name of Pooja Specify the name of Puja eg. Maha Mritunjay Path Capacity for the Puja How many people would be attending the Puja. Let’s say a single person, or a couple or a complete family of 4 people or more people Slots available Sellers can respond with the available slots which can specify date and time for the Puja. For example Maha Mritunjay Puja can be performed on 6th October from 4pm to 6pm Date of the Puja Time of the Puja Duration of subscription: The duration will be defined in the ISO format to enable a user to specify and answer- how long any particular subscription is needed for? P is the duration designator (for period) placed at the start of the duration representation. Y is the year designator that follows the value for the number of years. M is the month designator that follows the value for the number of months. W is the week designator that follows the value for the number of weeks. D is the day designator that follows the value for the number of days. T is the time designator that precedes the time components of the representation. 1 month duration can be presented as **P1M** 48 hours duration can be presented as **PT48H** 6 months duration can be presented as **P6M** Fulfilment type Online Puja: the Puja would be attended by the user in an online setup over a video call. Seller can send this as a part of the catalogue if the same service is offered by the seller Offline Puja: Seller fulfilled Puja In case the Puja is being performed at the Temple, Temple details can be mentioned as Temple Description Buyer fulfilled Puja Location of Puja The puja can be performed at the user provided address Add ons Add-ons such as a Potli or some Yantra which would be provided along with the Puja can be specified in this attribute. These will be paid add ons and would have a value attached to it. There can also be free add ons as a consultation astrology paper that is being provided free of cost along with the service Pincode: Conditional mandatory (will be provided for offline model at the buyer location) The seller app will in return provide the quotation of the product as selected by the buyer The best price available for the product selection if the chosen product for purchase is available or not Breakup of best offer price Discounted base price/Base price Taxes involved Convenience fee(if any) Discount applied(if any) Other charges(if any) Scenario 2: **Online model** Name of Pooja Specify the name of Puja eg. Maha Mritunjay Path Slots available Sellers can respond with the available slots which can specify date, time and duration for the Puja. For example Maha Mritunjay Puja can be performed on 6th October from 4pm to 6pm Date of the Puja Time of the Puja Duration of the Puja How long the Puja will take place for? This will be defined in hours for eg. Maha Mritunjay Puja for two days will be defined as 48 hours Add ons Add-ons such as a Potli or some Yantra which would be provided along with the Puja can be specified in this attribute. These will be paid add ons and would have a value attached to it. There can also be free add ons as a consultation astrology paper that is being provided free of cost along with the service Pincode: Conditional mandatory (in case add ons need to be delivered at the buyer’s address) The seller app will in return provide the quotation of the product as selected by the buyer The best price available for the product selection if the chosen product for purchase is available or not Breakup of best offer price Discounted base price/Base price Taxes involved Convenience fee(if any) Discount applied(if any) Other charges(if any) The next step would be to place the order and agree to the terms of agreement by both seller and buyer app Pass the user identifier along with the address while the order is being placed to the seller app **Payment and Confirmation of Order** The buyer will make the payment to confirm the order Payment can have three scenarios: Entire payment to be made pre-fulfilment. In this case the payment needs to be made before the order is placed. Entire payment to be made post-fulfilment. In this case the payment needs to be made post the order is placed and puja service delivered delivered Entire payment to be made on-fulfilment Payment can be collected by both the buyer and seller app Buyer app collecting payment: Buyer app will send the payment link to the buyer and collect payment Buyer app to send details for confirming order to the seller app depending on the method of payment Puja chosen details according to the select call transaction ID User Identifier: Phone number or email Once confirmed from the seller app, the Puja purchase would be mapped to the user Seller app collecting payment: While the seller app sends the terms of agreement for the sale to go through, the seller app will also provide the payment link along with the cancellation terms The buyer will make payment through the same link and order ID would be generated by the seller app The seller app will pass the order ID to the buyer app Post this the buyer app will map the Puja details to the user and save the same on the profile for the user **Post Order activities** Once the order is confirmed, the buyer and seller will take relevant actions as per the terms of the order All the steps to be taken to provide the service of the Puja will be done at the seller app’s end. The buyer app has to maintain only the status of the order to provide the buyer an informed decision about the updates for his purchase Puja details to be visible to the user on Buyer Platform under the user profile section In case the Puja is being delivered online/offline on different dates, below scenarios are possible. Scenario 1: Fulfilment Type- Offline Puja Seller app which is taking care of delivery(both online and offline) which is in this case is offline delivery of service of Puja, needs to update buyer app for keeping track of the service This call can have 3 statuses for order Accepted: Once the seller app accepts the order In- Progress: Puja service is in progress Completed: When the Puja service order is completed As and when actual delivery is completed for the Puja service ,seller app to send completed to mark the delivery completion of the puja service On the other hand, a user can also request for status of the product. In this case, buyer app to send a /status call and receive the /on_status from seller app to inform the user |
| **Alternate Path**        | In case the payment fails on the seller app, below use cases are possible in that case: Use case 1 \- Redirection and timed out When the seller app is collecting the payment and there happens to be a timeout error as the buyer failed to make the payment within the specified time limit: Buyer app would have not received a confirmation on the order In this case post completion of TAT for payment confirmation, seller app needs to do an unsolicited call to the buyer app informing about the error in payment Error: Payment Timed Out Post this the buyer app can reinitiate payment with the buyer(/init call) When the new payment is initiated by the buyer app, the seller app will generate a new payment link and sent across to the buyer app and reinitiation of order payment takes place Use case 3 \- Payment link not timed out but the buyer app makes a /Status call to the seller app When the seller app is collecting the payment and there happens to be a payment failure at the seller app’s end: Buyer app can make a status call to get the updated status of order Buyer app would have not received a confirmation on the order In this case, the buyer app will send a request to the seller app of not receiving a payment confirmation to which the seller app will inform back with an error: Error: Payment failure Or Error: Mandate setup failure Post this the buyer can reinitiate payment for the purchase by connecting with the buyer and restarting the payment process There will be other use cases, these are just a few examples. | **Alternate Path**        | If there is a change in address at the time of order confirmation In this case when the buyer wants to change the address of the service delivery The buyer app will facilitate the buyer to change the address for the order Once the new address is captured, the buyer app will make an update call to the seller app for address change The seller app on receiving the new address, three scenarios can be possible **The seller app does not service the new address location**: Inform the buyer app that service is not possible for the new location and relay the same information to the buyer **The address is updated without a change in price:** Seller app updates the address and informs the buyer app regarding the same. The buyer app relays the same response to the buyer The new address is captured on the buyer app **There is a change of price for address updation** On receiving the new address through the buyer app, the seller app will send across a new payment link in the update order response Buyer app to relay the payment link to the buyer Once the payment is received from the buyer, buyer app to relay the same response to the seller app and accordingly the seller app will facilitate the service of the Puja Buyer app to update the address for the service at it’s end for the buyer’s visibility | **Alternate Path**        | Future Use Case: Remedies/offerings selection by buyer in the middle of the Puja For example at the time of puja at the buyer’s location, there is the need of a Havan Kund which the seller is carrying along but was not added in the original order For example, at the time of Puja at the buyer’s location, the pandit offers a Rudraksh mala as an added remedy for the puja and the buyer decides to purchase it This is an update to the original order and will be handled on the protocol | Use Case 2: Astrology Services | Buyer raises a request for Astrology services on a buyer app → Seller responds with available astrology services details→ Buyer selects an astrology service and fulfilment method(chat, call, video) → Seller confirms the appointment → Puja is conducted as per the chosen details. | Actor                          | \*\*Buyer (one with the need)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |     | Seller (one with the inventory) |     | Buyer app |     | Seller app\*\* |
| Main Path                      | **Thought** Astrology services offer valuable guidance and insights into various aspects of life, including career, relationships, and personal well-being. By utilising the wisdom of astrology, individuals can make more informed decisions and find clarity in challenging situations. ONDC is working to make astrology services interoperable across its network, ensuring that users have seamless access to trusted astrologers, regardless of their platform, and can benefit from personalised consultations to meet their unique needs. **Initiate Buyer’s Request** Buyer’s request for any Spirituality related product can be raised through the buyer app in three possible ways: Search through category: Buyer can easily search for the category directly such as Astrology service Search by city: Buyer app can raise a search request by city for eg. all sellers selling only in Lucknow For explanation purposes, search by category is defined here. Search by category: Buyer on the buyer app raises an intent to purchase an astrology service of either of the following, Astrology Services Puja Services The buyer can raise an intent of either one of the above or all of the above categories of spirituality services available **Broadcast to Sellers** The interest is broadcasted to all the available sellers in the specific domain on the ONDC network via the gateway **Seller responds with their catalogue** Sellers will respond with their catalogues with **attributes** for the buyer app to define the discovery experience for the buyer. These attributes will be needed as selection from the buyer to define the quote of a purchasable item. The different attributes defined are: Service or Concern: Sellers can respond with Service or Concern to specify the type of E Puja services they offer, such as career related Puja or Relationship Related Puja These will be enums as defined below: Career Marriage Love Energy Home Education Job Astrologer for the consultation: Sellers can respond with a list of astrologers based on their specialties, ratings, and experience. Astrologer’s photo can also be passed as an added attribute for the buyer to take an informed decision Language of Astrologer: Sellers can respond with languages that the Pandit speaks based on preferred languages (e.g., Hindi, English, Kannada) Experience of Astrologer: Sellers can respond with the experience level of each Astrologer, helping them select a knowledgeable professional. This can be in years eg. 10+ years, 12+ years Education/Qualification of Astrologer: Any eligibility certification can be specified for this attribute Slots available: Sellers will respond with available slots which can specify date and time. For example, call consultation with Dr. Ajai Bhambi costs Rs.500 on 15th Oct at 6PM Date of astro consult Time of astro consult Form for User Details: A form to collect necessary user information can be shared by the seller (e.g., name, contact number, birth details, Gotra) Fulfilment type Chat consultation: Where the astrologer consults on chat with the buyer Call consultation: Where the astrologer consults on call with the buyer Video consultation: Where the astrologer consults on a video call with the buyer Add ons: Add-ons such as a Potli or some Yantra which would be provided along with the Puja can be specified in this attribute. These will be paid add ons and would have a value attached to it. There can also be free add ons as a consultation astrology paper that is being provided free of cost along with the service Description of Astrology service: Any further details related to the Puja that the seller deems fit for the user to be aware of can be passed in this attribute. As birth details are compulsory for Kundali generation. Image of Astrology service: This can also be passed as a part of seller’s catalogue Credentials of Astrologer Any certificates that the Seller app understands are important to verify the authenticity for the seller can be added for this attribute Certificate name Certification number to check the authenticity Rating from seller Seller can pass the rating related to the any astrology service so that the buyer can take an informed decision regarding purchase of the service **Offer Management & Selection** Buyer will select the most suitable astrology service that they deem fit for their usage from all seller Apps catalogue Different models to be present for selection as received in the catalogue sent by the seller. Scenario 1: **Online fulfilment model** Let’s suppose the seller app offers online chat or call or video consultation The buyer app will have to provide details related to the selection for the seller to provide a quote. This will include: Service or concern: The issue for which consultation services are being taken eg. marital issues, love concerns Astrologer selected Specify the name of Astrologer eg. Dr. Ajai Bhambi Slot chosen Buyer’s selection for the available slot. For example Astrologer eg. Dr. Rs.500 on 15th Oct at 6PM Attributes available within slot to define the duration correctly are: Date of the consultation Time of the consultation Fulfilment type Chat consultation: Where the astrologer consults on chat with the buyer For chat consultation, the chat window link between the astrologer and the buyer will be send across through the protocol to the buyer app by the seller app Call consultation: Where the astrologer consults on call with the buyer app, the buyer app to provide the phone number to the seller app for establishing a secure connection by the seller app through third party applications like Ameyo, etc. Video consultation: Where the astrologer consults on a video call with the buyer. The video chat room link would be passed through the protocol to the buyer app where the buyer would be redirected. The consultation links need to be passed through the protocol to the buyer app from the seller app. Form for buyer details: If the seller has requested any extra details for the consultation, such as birth details, gotra, etc, buyer will have to provide the same Add ons Add-ons such as a Potli or some Yantra which would be provided along with the Puja can be specified in this attribute. These will be paid add ons and would have a value attached to it. There can also be free add ons as a consultation astrology paper that is being provided free of cost along with the service Pincode: Conditional mandatory (will be provided for offline model) The seller app will in return provide the quotation of the product as selected by the buyer The best price available for the product selection if the chosen product for purchase is available or not Breakup of best offer price Discounted base price/Base price Taxes involved Convenience fee(if any) Discount applied(if any) Other charges(if any) The next step would be to place the order and agree to the terms of agreement by both seller and buyer app Pass the user identifier along with the address while the order is being placed to the seller app **Payment and Confirmation of Order** The buyer will make the payment to confirm the order Payment can have three scenarios: Entire payment to be made pre-fulfilment. In this case the payment needs to be made before the order is placed. Entire payment to be made post-fulfilment. In this case the payment needs to be made post the order is placed and astrology service delivered Entire payment to be made on-fulfilment Payment can be collected by both the buyer and seller app Buyer app collecting payment: Buyer app will send the payment link to the buyer and collect payment Buyer app to send details for confirming order to the seller app depending on the method of payment Astrology service chosen details according to the select call transaction ID User Identifier: Phone number or email Once confirmed from the seller app, the astrology service purchase would be mapped to the user Seller app collecting payment: While the seller app sends the terms of agreement for the sale to go through, the seller app will also provide the payment link along with the cancellation terms The buyer will make payment through the same link and order ID would be generated by the seller app The seller app will pass the order ID to the buyer app Post this the buyer app will map the astrology service details to the user and save the same on the profile for the user **Post Order activities** Once the order is confirmed, the buyer and seller will take relevant actions as per the terms of the order All the steps to be taken to provide the service of the Puja will be done at the buyer app’s end. Astrology service details to be visible to the user on Buyer Platform under the user profile section In case the Puja is being delivered online, below scenarios are possible. Scenario 1: Fulfilment Type- Chat Once the order confirmation has been done, seller app to provide a chat link in the order confirmation call so that the buyer app can redirect the buyer to the link where chat consultation will be provided This call can have 3 statuses for order Accepted: Once the seller app accepts the order In- Progress: astro consultation service is in progress Completed: When the astrology service is completed As and when actual delivery is completed for the astro consultation service ,buyer app to send completed to mark the delivery completion of the puja service Scenario 2: Fulfilment Type- Call Once the order confirmation has been done, seller app to provide a **phone** **call link** in the order confirmation call so that the buyer app can redirect the buyer to the link where consultation will be provided This call can have 3 statuses for order Accepted: Once the seller app accepts the order In- Progress: astro consultation service is in progress Completed: When the astrology service is completed As and when actual delivery is completed for the Puja service ,buyer app to send completed to mark the delivery completion of the puja service Scenario 3: Fulfilment Type- Video Once the order confirmation has been done, seller app to provide a **video chat link** in the order confirmation call so that the buyer app can redirect the buyer to the link where consultation will be provided This call can have 3 statuses for order Accepted: Once the seller app accepts the order In- Progress: astro consultation service is in progress Completed: When the astrology service is completed As and when actual delivery is completed for the Puja service ,buyer app to send completed to mark the delivery completion of the puja service If the buyer app fails to provide order completion status at the time of service completion, the seller app can make an unsolicited status call to get an update regarding the status of consultation. Scenario 1: Consultation incomplete In case the consultation is incomplete due to any of the below mentioned reasons, when the seller app does the status call, buyer app to inform the seller for incomplete consultation User did not join the consultation Astrologer did not join the consultation Time out error Scenario 2: If the consultation is successfully completed by then, buyer app to update the status to seller app |
| **Alternate Path**             | Consultation chat has inappropriate words that the buyer app cannot show across to the buyer On identification of such inappropriate chats, the buyer app will send across an error code to the seller app informing about inappropriate conversation cancellation and reschedule terms needs to be mentioned by the seller app through the protocol and same to be informed to the buyer through the buyer app so that the buyer can take an informed decision If the buyer still selects to go ahead with another astrologer, the buyer app will act on the cancellation terms and a place a new order for the other astrologer’s consultation being requested
